### How to use skills
- Discovery: The list above is the skills available in this session (name + description + file path). Skill bodies live on disk at the listed paths.
- Trigger rules: If the user names a skill (with $SkillName or plain text) OR the task clearly matches a skill's description shown above, you must use that skill for that turn. Multiple mentions mean use them all. Do not carry skills across turns unless re-mentioned.
- Missing/blocked: If a named skill isn't in the list or the path can't be read, say so briefly and continue with the best fallback.
- How to use a skill (progressive disclosure):
1) After deciding to use a skill, open its SKILL.md. Read only enough to follow the workflow.
2) When SKILL.md references relative paths (e.g., scripts/foo.py), resolve them relative to the skill directory listed above first, and only consider other paths if needed.
3) If SKILL.md points to extra folders such as references/, load only the specific files needed for the request; don't bulk-load everything.
4) If scripts/ exist, prefer running or patching them instead of retyping large code blocks.
5) If assets/ or templates exist, reuse them instead of recreating from scratch.
- Coordination and sequencing:
- If multiple skills apply, choose the minimal set that covers the request and state the order you'll use them.
- Announce which skill(s) you're using and why (one short line). If you skip an obvious skill, say why.
- Context hygiene:
- Keep context small: summarize long sections instead of pasting them; only load extra files when needed.
- Avoid deep reference-chasing: prefer opening only files directly linked from SKILL.md unless you're blocked.
- When variants exist (frameworks, providers, domains), pick only the relevant reference file(s) and note that choice.
- Safety and fallback: If a skill can't be applied cleanly (missing files, unclear instructions), state the issue, pick the next-best approach, and continue.

# AGENTS.md

## 读取顺序

## Instruction Priority

Superpowers skills override default system prompt behavior, but **user instructions always take precedence**:

1. **User's explicit instructions** (CLAUDE.md, GEMINI.md, AGENTS.md, direct requests) 鈥?highest priority
2. **Superpowers skills** 鈥?override default system behavior where they conflict
3. **Default system prompt** 鈥?lowest priority

If CLAUDE.md, GEMINI.md, or AGENTS.md says "don't use TDD" and a skill says "always use TDD," follow the user's instructions. The user is in control.

## How to Access Skills

**In Claude Code:** Use the `Skill` tool. When you invoke a skill, its content is loaded and presented to you鈥攆ollow it directly. Never use the Read tool on skill files.

**In Gemini CLI:** Skills activate via the `activate_skill` tool. Gemini loads skill metadata at session start and activates the full content on demand.

**In other environments:** Check your platform's documentation for how skills are loaded.

## Platform Adaptation

Skills use Claude Code tool names. Non-CC platforms: see `references/codex-tools.md` (Codex) for tool equivalents. Gemini CLI users get the tool mapping loaded automatically via GEMINI.md.

# Using Skills

## The Rule

**Invoke relevant or requested skills BEFORE any response or action.** Even a 1% chance a skill might apply means that you should invoke the skill to check. If an invoked skill turns out to be wrong for the situation, you don't need to use it.

```dot
digraph skill_flow {
    "User message received" [shape=doublecircle];
    "About to EnterPlanMode?" [shape=doublecircle];
    "Already brainstormed?" [shape=diamond];
    "Invoke brainstorming skill" [shape=box];
    "Might any skill apply?" [shape=diamond];
    "Invoke Skill tool" [shape=box];
    "Announce: 'Using [skill] to [purpose]'" [shape=box];
    "Has checklist?" [shape=diamond];
    "Create TodoWrite todo per item" [shape=box];
    "Follow skill exactly" [shape=box];
    "Respond (including clarifications)" [shape=doublecircle];

    "About to EnterPlanMode?" -> "Already brainstormed?";
    "Already brainstormed?" -> "Invoke brainstorming skill" [label="no"];
    "Already brainstormed?" -> "Might any skill apply?" [label="yes"];
    "Invoke brainstorming skill" -> "Might any skill apply?";

    "User message received" -> "Might any skill apply?";
    "Might any skill apply?" -> "Invoke Skill tool" [label="yes, even 1%"];
    "Might any skill apply?" -> "Respond (including clarifications)" [label="definitely not"];
    "Invoke Skill tool" -> "Announce: 'Using [skill] to [purpose]'";
    "Announce: 'Using [skill] to [purpose]'" -> "Has checklist?";
    "Has checklist?" -> "Create TodoWrite todo per item" [label="yes"];
    "Has checklist?" -> "Follow skill exactly" [label="no"];
    "Create TodoWrite todo per item" -> "Follow skill exactly";
}
```

## Red Flags

These thoughts mean STOP鈥攜ou're rationalizing:

| Thought | Reality |
|---------|---------|
| "This is just a simple question" | Questions are tasks. Check for skills. |
| "I need more context first" | Skill check comes BEFORE clarifying questions. |
| "Let me explore the codebase first" | Skills tell you HOW to explore. Check first. |
| "I can check git/files quickly" | Files lack conversation context. Check for skills. |
| "Let me gather information first" | Skills tell you HOW to gather information. |
| "This doesn't need a formal skill" | If a skill exists, use it. |
| "I remember this skill" | Skills evolve. Read current version. |
| "This doesn't count as a task" | Action = task. Check for skills. |
| "The skill is overkill" | Simple things become complex. Use it. |
| "I'll just do this one thing first" | Check BEFORE doing anything. |
| "This feels productive" | Undisciplined action wastes time. Skills prevent this. |
| "I know what that means" | Knowing the concept 鈮?using the skill. Invoke it. |

## Skill Priority

When multiple skills could apply, use this order:

1. **Process skills first** (brainstorming, debugging) - these determine HOW to approach the task
2. **Implementation skills second** (frontend-design, mcp-builder) - these guide execution

"Let's build X" 鈫?brainstorming first, then implementation skills.
"Fix this bug" 鈫?debugging first, then domain-specific skills.

## Skill Types

**Rigid** (TDD, debugging): Follow exactly. Don't adapt away discipline.

**Flexible** (patterns): Adapt principles to context.

The skill itself tells you which.

## User Instructions

Instructions say WHAT, not HOW. "Add X" or "Fix Y" doesn't mean skip workflows.

description: Detect, initialize, and maintain a reusable MemoryTree project-memory workspace for any code repository. On activation, immediately detect and report the repo's MemoryTree state.

# MemoryTree

Use this skill for repo-level project memory. Do not treat it as an application runtime feature unless the user explicitly asks to productize it.

## On Activation

When this skill is invoked, immediately perform these steps without waiting for further user input:

1. Detect the repo state (`not-installed`, `partial`, or `installed`) using `references/project-detection.md`.
2. Check `~/.memorytree/alerts.json`. If pending alerts exist, display them to the user before proceeding.
3. If `not-installed`: run `memorytree init` to scaffold the workspace, then report what was created.
4. If `partial`: run `memorytree upgrade` to add missing pieces, then report what was added.
5. If `installed`: read the active goal, bound todo, and latest chat log. Report the current state (goal summary, todo progress, pending tasks) and ask the user what they want to work on next. Before recommending daemon setup, verify that the resolved `memorytree` command is real and healthy. When the command is missing, silent, zero-byte, or resolves into an unrelated install directory, run `node <installed-skill-root>/dist/cli.js doctor` and fall back to direct `node <installed-skill-root>/dist/cli.js ...` invocation instead of repeating the broken global command. If `memorytree daemon status` shows the heartbeat is not registered and command resolution is healthy, ask the user whether they want the recommended current-repository setup via `memorytree daemon quick-start --root <repo>` or only a machine-level scheduler restore via `memorytree daemon install --interval 5m --auto-push true`. Use `memorytree daemon register` only when they explicitly want custom branch, interval, report-port, or worktree settings. Use plain-text questions compatible with all AI assistants, not client-specific UI components.

Do not stop after detection to ask whether you should proceed. Act on the result immediately.

## Core Behavior

1. Detect the repo state before changing files. Use `references/project-detection.md`.
2. If MemoryTree is missing, initialize it with `memorytree init`. If the CLI is not available, create the files from `assets/templates/`.
3. If MemoryTree is partial, upgrade it with `memorytree upgrade` before manual maintenance.
4. If MemoryTree is already installed, maintain only the active goal, bound todo, and current chat log. Use `references/update-rules.md`.
5. Keep the installation compatible with the host repo's branch, PR, CI, and review rules. Use `references/git-policy.md`.
6. Prefer safe defaults: do not add reply suffix requirements unless the host repository already requires them, do not mix code-and-memory commits by default, and do not override branch policy. MemoryTree-only git automation is allowed only inside the isolated flow in `references/git-policy.md`.
7. When locale is not explicit, choose it from repo language first, then system language. Use `references/locale-selection.md`.
8. Keep reply language aligned with user language first, then repo locale. Use `references/response-language.md`.
9. For partial repos, use the non-destructive upgrade path before manual maintenance. Use `references/upgrade-path.md`.
10. When transcript archival is enabled, import transcripts with deterministic code, preserve raw transcripts as evidence in both the current repo mirror and the global archive, generate cleaned Markdown for indexing, keep cross-project backfills and ambiguous ownership cases in the global archive only, and ask once per repository whether raw transcript files may be committed or pushed. Use `references/transcript-archive.md`.
11. When CLI commands are needed, use `memorytree <subcommand>` (requires Node.js 鈮?20). If Node.js is not available, fall back to manual scaffolding from `assets/templates/`. See `references/execution-environment.md`.
12. Transcript discovery, import, cleaning, and push are handled by the background heartbeat process. The model only writes chat log summaries and updates goals and todos. See `references/heartbeat-scheduling.md`.
13. Global configuration is stored in `~/.memorytree/config.toml`. See `references/global-configuration.md`.
14. When the user asks to see their most recent conversation, trigger an on-demand transcript sync for the current project, locate the latest session across all three clients, and generate a continuation summary. See `references/transcript-archive.md` and `references/heartbeat-scheduling.md`.
15. All interactive prompts (heartbeat install, configuration, session continuity) must use plain-text questions compatible with every AI assistant that supports this skill. Do not rely on client-specific UI components. See `references/heartbeat-scheduling.md`.

## Read Order

1. Repo `AGENTS.md`, if present.
2. Latest file in `Memory/01_goals/`.
3. Latest todo bound to that goal in `Memory/02_todos/`.
4. `Memory/04_knowledge/` only when needed.
5. `Memory/06_transcripts/clean/`, transcript manifests, and repo-local raw transcript mirrors only when transcript history or cross-project memory search is relevant.
6. `Memory/03_chat_logs/` and `Memory/05_archive/` only when needed.

## Detect

1. Check whether `Memory/` exists and matches the layout in `references/memory-layout.md`.
2. Classify the repo as `not-installed`, `partial`, or `installed`.
3. If the repo already has stronger rules than the generated templates, preserve the repo rules and only add missing MemoryTree pieces.

## Upgrade

1. Use `memorytree upgrade` for repositories that already have `AGENTS.md`, custom policy files, or partial `Memory/` content.
2. Preserve existing repo policy files by default.
3. Create only the missing MemoryTree pieces.
4. Read the upgrade result and treat `agents_merge_required=true` as a manual review task, not an overwrite instruction.

## Initialize

1. Run `memorytree init --root <repo>` and pass `--project-name`, `--goal-summary`, and `--locale` when the user already provided them.
2. Use fresh init only when the repo does not already have `AGENTS.md` or another repo policy source such as a policy-bearing `CONTRIBUTING.md`, PR templates, `CODEOWNERS`, or commitlint config. If repo policy already exists, switch to `memorytree upgrade` instead of trying to skip `AGENTS.md`.
3. Review the generated `AGENTS.md` before keeping it. Merge it with the repo's existing policy if needed.
4. Keep the initial installation minimal: `Memory/01_goals`, `02_todos`, `03_chat_logs`, optional `04_knowledge`, `05_archive`, and `06_transcripts` only when transcript archival is enabled for the repo or needed for transcript import.
5. Use the locale-specific template files in `assets/templates/<locale>/` as the source of truth for first-run scaffolding.
6. Prefer `--locale auto` when the user did not request a language explicitly.
7. Use `memorytree locale` when you need a deterministic locale check without scaffolding files.
8. If Node.js is not available, create first-run files directly from `assets/templates/` instead of requiring a runtime installation.
9. If transcript archival is enabled for the repo, use `memorytree import --source <file>` for one explicit source file and `memorytree discover` when scanning local client stores. Matching transcripts must update both the repo mirror and the global archive, while unrelated projects, ambiguous ownership cases, or mismatched explicit sources are archived in the global archive only. Let the CLI generate cleaned transcripts deterministically without spending model tokens on the cleaning step.
10. Ask once whether raw transcript files may also be committed to the repository. Record the answer in `AGENTS.md`, keep the files in the repo either way, and exclude `raw` files from automatic staging until the user says yes.

## Maintain

1. Change the active goal only after explicit user confirmation of a scope or requirement change.
2. Update the active todo when progress changes, milestones move, or the next task becomes clearer.
3. Append chat logs only. Never rewrite or delete prior entries.
4. Keep active files small. Move stale context to archive or knowledge files instead of bloating the active goal or todo.
5. Treat product ideas, architecture decisions, and operating constraints as goal or knowledge content. Treat step-by-step execution state as todo content.
6. Treat cleaned transcript indexes as discovery aids, not as the final source of truth. When exact wording matters, confirm against the raw transcript archive.
7. Prefer deterministic CLI-based transcript cleaning over manual rewriting. Do not spend model tokens to restate or normalize transcript content when `memorytree import` can do it.
8. Reply in the user's language when clear; otherwise align with repo locale without rewriting existing files just to translate them.

## Git And Safety

1. Never assume MemoryTree can override the repo's branch model.
2. Default to isolated MemoryTree-only Git operations: stage only MemoryTree-owned files, use a MemoryTree-scoped commit title, push to a dedicated branch, and open a dedicated PR.
3. Enable auto-merge only for MemoryTree-only PRs, and only when the repository still enforces its required review and CI checks.
4. Keep repo-local raw transcript mirrors and the global transcript archive synchronized on every import. The global index must remain safe for concurrent multi-project updates.
5. Keep the repository mirror limited to transcripts that belong to the current repository. Unrelated or ambiguous transcripts belong in the global archive only.
6. Keep raw transcript files under `Memory/06_transcripts/raw/**` in the repo, but exclude them from automatic staging until the user explicitly approved raw transcript uploads for that repository.
7. If the diff mixes product code, shared policy files, cross-project transcript archives, or unclear ownership, stop and ask the user before committing or pushing.
8. If the repo has protected branches or PR-only rules, follow them even if older MemoryTree rules say otherwise.
9. When `auto_push` is enabled, the heartbeat process pushes automatically after committing. If no Git remote is configured, the push is skipped. If a push fails, the heartbeat retries once. In either case an alert is written to `~/.memorytree/alerts.json`. See `references/git-policy.md`.
10. During transcript cleaning, the heartbeat scans for sensitive information (API keys, passwords, tokens). Matches are logged as warnings only 鈥?no automatic deletion or redaction. See `references/heartbeat-scheduling.md`.

11. Do not modify the host repository's CI or E2E workflow definitions by default. If the user explicitly approves a MemoryTree-only optimization, prefer path-filtered or lightweight workflows for `Memory/**` and managed `AGENTS.md` PRs without weakening required branch protection.

## Resources

- `references/project-detection.md`: detect install state and choose init vs maintain.
- `references/memory-layout.md`: folder and file naming rules.
- `references/update-rules.md`: when to version goals, todos, and session logs.
- `references/git-policy.md`: safe Git defaults and policy merge guidance.
- `references/locale-selection.md`: locale choice rules and alias behavior.
- `references/response-language.md`: reply-language precedence and translation safety.
- `references/transcript-archive.md`: raw transcript archival, clean transcript indexing, per-client source rules, and repo upload confirmation rules.
- `references/upgrade-path.md`: safe adoption flow for partial repos.
- `references/execution-environment.md`: how to run MemoryTree CLI (requires Node.js 鈮?20).
- `references/heartbeat-scheduling.md`: background heartbeat architecture, daemon CLI, and execution flow.
- `references/global-configuration.md`: `~/.memorytree/` directory layout, `config.toml` schema, and `alerts.json` format.
- `assets/templates/en/` and `assets/templates/zh-cn/`: seed files for English and Simplified Chinese initialization.
- CLI commands: `memorytree init`, `memorytree upgrade`, `memorytree import`, `memorytree discover`, `memorytree locale`, `memorytree recall`, `memorytree doctor`, `memorytree daemon install|uninstall|run-once|watch|status|quick-start|register`.

# Project Detection

Use this file before changing any MemoryTree files.

## States

### `not-installed`

Treat the repo as `not-installed` when any of these are true:

- No `Memory/` directory exists.
- No `AGENTS.md` exists and there are no active goal, bound todo, or chat-log files to preserve.

Action:

1. Run `scripts/init-memorytree.py`.
2. Review the generated files.
3. Use fresh init only when there is no `AGENTS.md` or other repo policy source to preserve. If repo policy already exists, switch to `scripts/upgrade-memorytree.py`.

### `partial`

Treat the repo as `partial` when MemoryTree exists but one or more expected pieces are missing:

- `Memory/` exists but one of `01_goals`, `02_todos`, or `03_chat_logs` is missing.
- `AGENTS.md` already exists even if `Memory/` does not yet exist. Use upgrade to avoid overwriting repo policy.
- Common repo policy sources already exist, such as policy-bearing `CONTRIBUTING.md`, PR templates, `CODEOWNERS`, or commitlint config. Use upgrade to avoid conflicting Git guidance.
- Goal files exist but there is no bound todo for the latest goal.
- A chat-log directory exists but no current chat-log file exists.
- `AGENTS.md` is missing or does not mention the MemoryTree read order, isolated commit/PR flow, and safety rules.

Action:

1. Run `scripts/upgrade-memorytree.py`.
2. Preserve stricter repo policies already present in `AGENTS.md`.

### `installed`

Treat the repo as `installed` when these are all true:

- `Memory/01_goals/`, `Memory/02_todos/`, and `Memory/03_chat_logs/` exist.
- At least one goal file exists.
- At least one todo file bound to the latest goal exists.
- At least one current chat-log file exists.
- `AGENTS.md` exists and already carries MemoryTree read-order, isolated commit/PR, and safety guidance.

Action:

1. Read active files in order.
2. Update only the active goal, active todo, and current session log as needed.

## Detection Notes

- Do not require `04_knowledge` or `05_archive` for a valid install.
- Do not require `06_transcripts/` for a valid install. Transcript archival is optional; when enabled, keep the current-project mirror and the user-level global archive synchronized together.
- Fresh init now checks common non-`AGENTS.md` policy files such as PR templates, `CODEOWNERS`, commitlint config, and policy-bearing `CONTRIBUTING.md`. Generic contributor docs without Git or PR rules do not block fresh init by themselves.
- Do not replace an existing `AGENTS.md` blindly. Merge carefully.
- If the repo already has its own memory system, ask before adding a second one.

- 方案B Phase 0：冻结边界与执行口径，文档化“单一路径、禁止旧架构级兜底、保留明确报错保护、worker 内常驻预热”的新设计。
- 方案B Phase 1 准备启动：按测试和 `domain/video/pipeline.py` 的目标接口重建 `domain/video/stages/`，并先补最小可运行骨架；后续在主链收敛后建立平台无关 API/CLI 和多平台 skill 适配层。

## 已完成
- 已确认当前真实运行链仍由 `domain/video/pre/main/pipeline.py` 驱动，OpenClaw 已可通过现有 API/worker 跑通真实 `test.mp4`。
- 已在 Windows 宿主机安装并跑通本地 Redis，当前 API 已运行在 Redis 队列/注册模式。
- 已完成结果协议首轮收敛，OpenClaw 可获取 `openclaw_result` 与关键 artifacts。
- 已验证 warm runner 能显著减少“每任务重新起解释器”的额外开销，但该方案仅作为上一阶段试验结果保留，不进入方案B主设计。
- 已重建 `.venv-p310` 运行环境，并修复旧 `pre` 内置流水线在新环境下的两个关键运行时问题：子进程输出编码导致的 warm runner 失败，以及 `ffmpeg` 隐式路径依赖导致的 step6 中断；`test.mp4` 已于 2026-03-27 通过 OpenClaw -> CloneCut -> 回传链路再次验证，结果为 `executed_mode=real_pipeline`。

## 待完成
- 重建 `domain/video/stages/base.py`、`utils.py` 与各 stage 模块，恢复 `domain.video.pipeline` 的可导入与可测试状态。

- 将 ASR、VideoClipper、字幕处理、封面渲染等重资源收敛为 worker 进程内常驻资源，并补齐并发治理与 ready 信号。
- 修改 `apps/worker/service.py`，让通用视频任务主路径直接调用 `VideoPipeline`。
- 建立平台无关 API/CLI 通用入口，让任何支持 skill/tool/shell/MCP 的平台都可以复用 CloneCut 能力。
- 让 OpenClaw skill 改为调用通用入口，而不是直接绑定内部实现；并预留其他平台 skill/wrapper 的接入方式。
- 用 OpenClaw 重新完成 `test.mp4` 端到端验证，并确认主成片、字幕、封面、脚本、日志回传稳定。
- 清理旧 `pre/main/pipeline.py` 在 worker 主路径上的运行时依赖，并单独决策 `ExternalVideoCommandAdapter` 是迁移期兼容还是正式废弃。

from __future__ import annotations

from dataclasses import dataclass, field
import logging
from pathlib import Path
from typing import Any, Callable, Dict, List, Optional

from domain.video.config import VideoPipelineConfig
from domain.video.stages import (
    run_stage0_clean,
    run_stage1_transcode,
    run_stage2_silence,
    run_stage3_repair,
    run_stage4_asr,
    run_stage5_ai_text,
    run_stage6_5_resub,
    run_stage6_clip,
    run_stage7_correct,
    run_stage7_subtitle,
    run_stage8_cover,
    run_stage9_organize,
)
from domain.video.stages.base import StageResult
from domain.video.stages.utils import probe_duration_seconds


@dataclass
class PipelineResult:
    success: bool
    output_file: Optional[str] = None
    error_message: Optional[str] = None
    executed_stages: List[str] = field(default_factory=list)
    performance_summary: str = ""
    current_stage: int = 0
    last_stage: Optional[str] = None
    failed_stage: Optional[str] = None
    performance_report: Optional[Any] = None


class VideoPipeline:
    """Internal multi-stage video pipeline."""

    def __init__(
        self,
        config: VideoPipelineConfig,
        logger: Optional[logging.Logger] = None,
        performance_tracker: Any = None,
        resource_monitor: Any = None,
    ) -> None:
        self.config = config
        self.logger = logger or logging.getLogger("clonecut.domain.video.pipeline")
        self.performance_tracker = performance_tracker
        self.resource_monitor = resource_monitor
        self._stages: List[tuple[str, Callable[..., StageResult]]] = [
            ("stage0_clean", self._stage0),
            ("stage1_transcode", self._stage1),
            ("stage2_silence", self._stage2),
            ("stage3_repair", self._stage3),
            ("stage4_asr", self._stage4),
            ("stage5_ai_text", self._stage5),
            ("stage6_clip", self._stage6),
            ("stage6_5_resub", self._stage6_5),
            ("stage7_correct", self._stage7_correct),
            ("stage7_subtitle", self._stage7),
            ("stage8_cover", self._stage8),
            ("stage9_organize", self._stage9),
        ]

    def run(
        self,
        input_video: str,
        task_id: str,
        start_from_stage: int = 0,
        forum_post_info: Optional[dict] = None,
    ) -> PipelineResult:
        current = input_video
        executed: List[str] = []
        stage_start = max(0, int(start_from_stage))
        context: Dict[str, Any] = {"forum_post_info": _normalize_forum_post_info(forum_post_info)}
        last_stage_index = max(0, min(stage_start, len(self._stages) - 1 if self._stages else 0))
        last_stage_name: Optional[str] = None
        gpu_stage_indexes = {1, 2, 4, 6}
        tracking_started = False

        if self.performance_tracker is not None:
            try:
                path = Path(input_video)
                file_size_mb = 0.0
                if path.exists():
                    file_size_mb = path.stat().st_size / (1024 * 1024)
                duration_seconds = probe_duration_seconds(input_video)
                self.performance_tracker.start_video_processing(
                    task_id=task_id,
                    video_filename=path.name,
                    original_filename=path.name,
                    file_size_mb=file_size_mb,
                    video_duration_seconds=duration_seconds,
                )
                tracking_started = True
            except Exception as exc:
                self.logger.warning("start performance tracking failed: task=%s err=%s", task_id, exc)

        for idx, (stage_name, handler) in enumerate(self._stages):
            if idx < stage_start:
                continue

            if self.resource_monitor is not None:
                try:
                    self.resource_monitor.record_step_resource(
                        step_num=idx,
                        step_name=stage_name,
                        task_id=task_id,
                    )
                except Exception as exc:
                    self.logger.debug("resource snapshot failed: task=%s stage=%s err=%s", task_id, stage_name, exc)
            if self.performance_tracker is not None:
                try:
                    self.performance_tracker.start_stage(
                        task_id=task_id,
                        stage_name=stage_name,
                        gpu_accelerated=(idx in gpu_stage_indexes),
                    )
                except Exception:
                    pass
            try:
                result = handler(current, task_id=task_id, stage_name=stage_name, context=context)
            except Exception as exc:
                if self.performance_tracker is not None:
                    try:
                        self.performance_tracker.end_stage(
                            task_id=task_id,
                            stage_name=stage_name,
                            success=False,
                            error_message=str(exc),
                        )
                        self.performance_tracker.add_error(task_id, str(exc))
                    except Exception:
                        pass
                perf_report = self._finish_tracking(task_id, tracking_started)
                return PipelineResult(
                    success=False,
                    output_file=current,
                    error_message=f"{stage_name} exception: {exc}",
                    executed_stages=executed,
                    current_stage=idx,
                    last_stage=last_stage_name,
                    failed_stage=stage_name,
                    performance_report=perf_report,
                )

            executed.append(stage_name)
            last_stage_index = idx
            last_stage_name = stage_name
            if not result.success:
                if self.performance_tracker is not None:
                    try:
                        self.performance_tracker.end_stage(
                            task_id=task_id,
                            stage_name=stage_name,
                            success=False,
                            error_message=str(result.error_message or ""),
                        )
                        self.performance_tracker.add_error(
                            task_id,
                            str(result.error_message or f"{stage_name} failed"),
                        )
                    except Exception:
                        pass
                perf_report = self._finish_tracking(task_id, tracking_started)
                return PipelineResult(
                    success=False,
                    output_file=current,
                    error_message=result.error_message or f"{stage_name} failed",
                    executed_stages=executed,
                    current_stage=idx,
                    last_stage=last_stage_name,
                    failed_stage=stage_name,
                    performance_report=perf_report,
                )
            if self.performance_tracker is not None:
                try:
                    self.performance_tracker.end_stage(
                        task_id=task_id,
                        stage_name=stage_name,
                        success=True,
                    )
                except Exception:
                    pass
            if result.output_file:
                current = result.output_file

        perf_report = self._finish_tracking(task_id, tracking_started)
        summary = f"internal pipeline executed stages={len(executed)}"
        if perf_report is not None:
            try:
                ratio = float(getattr(perf_report, "processing_speed_ratio", 0.0))
                if ratio > 0:
                    summary = f"internal pipeline executed stages={len(executed)} speed={ratio:.2f}x"
            except Exception:
                pass
        return PipelineResult(
            success=True,
            output_file=current,
            executed_stages=executed,
            performance_summary=summary,
            current_stage=last_stage_index,
            last_stage=last_stage_name,
            performance_report=perf_report,
        )

    def _finish_tracking(self, task_id: str, tracking_started: bool) -> Optional[Any]:
        if not tracking_started or self.performance_tracker is None:
            return None
        try:
            return self.performance_tracker.end_video_processing(task_id)
        except Exception:
            return None

    def _stage0(self, current: str, task_id: str, stage_name: str, context: Dict[str, Any]) -> StageResult:
        self.logger.debug("pipeline stage start: %s task=%s", stage_name, task_id)
        return run_stage0_clean(current, self.config.output_dir, task_id)

    def _stage1(self, current: str, task_id: str, stage_name: str, context: Dict[str, Any]) -> StageResult:
        self.logger.debug("pipeline stage start: %s task=%s", stage_name, task_id)
        return run_stage1_transcode(current, self.config.output_dir, task_id)

    def _stage2(self, current: str, task_id: str, stage_name: str, context: Dict[str, Any]) -> StageResult:
        self.logger.debug("pipeline stage start: %s task=%s", stage_name, task_id)
        return run_stage2_silence(current, self.config.output_dir, task_id)

    def _stage3(self, current: str, task_id: str, stage_name: str, context: Dict[str, Any]) -> StageResult:
        self.logger.debug("pipeline stage start: %s task=%s", stage_name, task_id)
        return run_stage3_repair(current, self.config.output_dir, task_id)

    def _stage4(self, current: str, task_id: str, stage_name: str, context: Dict[str, Any]) -> StageResult:
        self.logger.debug("pipeline stage start: %s task=%s", stage_name, task_id)
        forum_info = context.get("forum_post_info") or {}
        hotwords = _normalize_hotwords(forum_info.get("hotwords"))
        speaker = str(forum_info.get("speaker", "")).strip()
        return run_stage4_asr(
            current,
            self.config.output_dir,
            task_id,
            forum_post_info=forum_info,
            hotwords=hotwords,
            speaker=speaker,
        )

    def _stage5(self, current: str, task_id: str, stage_name: str, context: Dict[str, Any]) -> StageResult:
        self.logger.debug("pipeline stage start: %s task=%s", stage_name, task_id)
        return run_stage5_ai_text(
            current,
            self.config.output_dir,
            task_id,
            forum_post_info=context.get("forum_post_info") or {},
        )

    def _stage6(self, current: str, task_id: str, stage_name: str, context: Dict[str, Any]) -> StageResult:
        self.logger.debug("pipeline stage start: %s task=%s", stage_name, task_id)
        return run_stage6_clip(current, self.config.output_dir, task_id)

    def _stage6_5(self, current: str, task_id: str, stage_name: str, context: Dict[str, Any]) -> StageResult:
        self.logger.debug("pipeline stage start: %s task=%s", stage_name, task_id)
        return run_stage6_5_resub(current, self.config.output_dir, task_id)

    def _stage7_correct(self, current: str, task_id: str, stage_name: str, context: Dict[str, Any]) -> StageResult:
        self.logger.debug("pipeline stage start: %s task=%s", stage_name, task_id)
        return run_stage7_correct(current, self.config.output_dir, task_id)

    def _stage7(self, current: str, task_id: str, stage_name: str, context: Dict[str, Any]) -> StageResult:
        self.logger.debug("pipeline stage start: %s task=%s", stage_name, task_id)
        return run_stage7_subtitle(current, self.config.output_dir, task_id)

    def _stage8(self, current: str, task_id: str, stage_name: str, context: Dict[str, Any]) -> StageResult:
        self.logger.debug("pipeline stage start: %s task=%s", stage_name, task_id)
        forum_info = _normalize_forum_post_info(context.get("forum_post_info"))
        context["forum_post_info"] = forum_info
        return run_stage8_cover(
            current,
            self.config.output_dir,
            task_id,
            forum_post_info=forum_info,
        )

    def _stage9(self, current: str, task_id: str, stage_name: str, context: Dict[str, Any]) -> StageResult:
        self.logger.debug("pipeline stage start: %s task=%s", stage_name, task_id)
        forum_info = _normalize_forum_post_info(context.get("forum_post_info"))
        original_filename = str(forum_info.get("original_filename", "")).strip()
        return run_stage9_organize(
            current,
            output_dir=self.config.output_dir,
            task_id=task_id,
            keep_intermediate_files=self.config.keep_intermediate_files,
            forum_post_info=forum_info,
            original_filename=original_filename,
        )


def _normalize_forum_post_info(raw: Optional[dict]) -> Dict[str, Any]:
    if not isinstance(raw, dict):
        return {}

    info: Dict[str, Any] = dict(raw)
    hotwords = _normalize_hotwords(info.get("hotwords"))
    info["hotwords"] = hotwords

    speaker = _pick_first_text(
        info,
        keys=("speaker", "speaker_id", "spk", "target_speaker"),
    )
    if speaker:
        info["speaker"] = speaker

    cover_titles = _normalize_cover_titles(info.get("cover_titles"))
    cover_up = _pick_first_text(info, keys=("cover_title_up", "灏侀潰鏍囬涓?))
    cover_middle = _pick_first_text(info, keys=("cover_title_middle", "灏侀潰鏍囬涓?))
    cover_down = _pick_first_text(info, keys=("cover_title_down", "灏侀潰鏍囬涓?))

    if not cover_up and len(cover_titles) >= 1:
        cover_up = cover_titles[0]
    if not cover_middle and len(cover_titles) >= 2:
        cover_middle = cover_titles[1]
    if not cover_down and len(cover_titles) >= 3:
        cover_down = cover_titles[2]

    compact_titles = [item for item in (cover_up, cover_middle, cover_down) if item]
    if compact_titles:
        cover_titles = compact_titles

    info["cover_title_up"] = cover_up
    info["cover_title_middle"] = cover_middle
    info["cover_title_down"] = cover_down
    info["灏侀潰鏍囬涓?] = cover_up
    info["灏侀潰鏍囬涓?] = cover_middle
    info["灏侀潰鏍囬涓?] = cover_down
    info["cover_titles"] = cover_titles

    return info


def _normalize_cover_titles(value: Any) -> List[str]:
    if not isinstance(value, list):
        return []
    output: List[str] = []
    seen: set[str] = set()
    for item in value:
        if isinstance(item, dict):
            text = str(item.get("text", "")).strip()
        else:
            text = str(item or "").strip()
        normalized = " ".join(text.split())
        if not normalized:
            continue
        if normalized in seen:
            continue
        seen.add(normalized)
        output.append(normalized)
        if len(output) >= 3:
            break
    return output


def _normalize_hotwords(value: Any) -> List[str]:
    candidates: List[str] = []
    if isinstance(value, list):
        candidates = [str(item).strip() for item in value]
    elif isinstance(value, str):
        candidates = [item.strip() for item in value.replace("\uFF0C", ",").split(",")]

    output: List[str] = []
    seen: set[str] = set()
    for item in candidates:
        text = str(item or "").strip()
        if not text:
            continue
        dedup_key = text.lower()
        if dedup_key in seen:
            continue
        seen.add(dedup_key)
        output.append(text)
    return output


def _pick_first_text(info: Dict[str, Any], keys: tuple[str, ...]) -> str:
    for key in keys:
        value = str(info.get(key, "")).strip()
        if value:
            return value
    return ""

def test_pipeline_stage4_manifest_contains_forum_context(monkeypatch, tmp_path) -> None:  # type: ignore[no-untyped-def]

    sidecar.write_text(
        "\n".join(
            [
                "1",
                "00:00:00,000 --> 00:00:02,000",
                "pipeline context subtitle",
                "",
            ]
        ),
        encoding="utf-8",
    )
    monkeypatch.setenv("CLONECUT_ASR_SIDECAR_PATH", str(sidecar))

    cfg = VideoPipelineConfig(output_dir=str(tmp_path / "out"))
    pipeline = VideoPipeline(cfg)
    result = pipeline.run(
        input_video=str(source),
        task_id="video-ctx",
        forum_post_info={"hotwords": ["topic-a", "topic-b"], "speaker": "spk-1"},
    )

    assert result.success
    manifest = tmp_path / "out" / "video-ctx" / "_stages" / "video-ctx_stage4_asr_manifest.json"

    assert payload.get("hotwords") == ["topic-a", "topic-b"]

    assert payload.get("speaker") == "spk-1"

    stage_dir.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)

def run_stage3_repair(input_video: str, output_dir: str, task_id: str) -> StageResult:
    source = Path(input_video)

from __future__ import annotations

import json
import os
from pathlib import Path
from typing import Any, Dict, List, Optional

from .base import StageResult
from .utils import ensure_stage_dir


def run_stage4_asr(
    input_video: str,
    output_dir: str,
    task_id: str,
    *,
    forum_post_info: Optional[dict] = None,
    hotwords: Optional[List[str]] = None,
    speaker: Optional[str] = None,
) -> StageResult:
    source = Path(input_video)
    stage_dir = ensure_stage_dir(output_dir, task_id)
    if not source.exists():
        return StageResult(success=False, output_file=input_video, error_message="stage4 input missing")

    srt_path = stage_dir / f"{task_id}_stage4_asr_subtitles.srt"
    manifest_path = stage_dir / f"{task_id}_stage4_asr_manifest.json"

    engine = "stub_asr"
    sidecar_backend = os.getenv("CLONECUT_ASR_BACKEND", "").strip().lower()
    sidecar_path = Path(os.getenv("CLONECUT_ASR_SIDECAR_PATH", "")).expanduser()

    if sidecar_backend == "sidecar" and sidecar_path.exists():
        srt_path.write_text(sidecar_path.read_text(encoding="utf-8"), encoding="utf-8")
        engine = "sidecar_srt"
    else:
        srt_path.write_text(
            "1\n00:00:00,000 --> 00:00:01,000\nclonecut stage4 stub\n",
            encoding="utf-8",
        )

    normalized_hotwords = [str(item).strip() for item in (hotwords or []) if str(item).strip()]
    payload: Dict[str, Any] = {
        "engine": engine,
        "task_id": task_id,
        "input_video": str(source),
        "subtitle_file": str(srt_path),
        "hotwords": normalized_hotwords,
        "hotword_count": len(normalized_hotwords),
        "speaker": str(speaker or "").strip(),
        "forum_post_info": forum_post_info or {},
    }
    manifest_path.write_text(json.dumps(payload, ensure_ascii=False, indent=2), encoding="utf-8")

    return StageResult(
        success=True,
        output_file=str(source),
        artifacts={"subtitle_file": str(srt_path), "manifest_file": str(manifest_path)},
        metadata={"engine": engine},
    )

def run_stage5_ai_text(
    input_video: str,
    output_dir: str,
    task_id: str,
    *,
    forum_post_info: Optional[dict] = None,
) -> StageResult:
    source = Path(input_video)
    stage_dir = ensure_stage_dir(output_dir, task_id)
    if not source.exists():

from __future__ import annotations

import json
import shutil
from pathlib import Path
from typing import Optional

from .base import StageResult
from .utils import ensure_stage_dir


def run_stage9_organize(
    input_video: str,
    *,
    output_dir: str,
    task_id: str,
    keep_intermediate_files: bool,
    forum_post_info: Optional[dict] = None,
    original_filename: str = "",
) -> StageResult:
    source = Path(input_video)
    stage_dir = ensure_stage_dir(output_dir, task_id)
    if not source.exists():
        return StageResult(success=False, output_file=input_video, error_message="stage9 input missing")

    task_root = Path(output_dir) / task_id
    task_root.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
    final_output = task_root / f"{task_id}_final.mp4"
    if source.resolve() != final_output.resolve():
        shutil.copyfile(source, final_output)

    manifest_path = stage_dir / f"{task_id}_stage9_organize_manifest.json"
    payload = {
        "task_id": task_id,
        "final_output": str(final_output),
        "keep_intermediate_files": bool(keep_intermediate_files),
        "original_filename": str(original_filename or ""),
        "forum_post_info": forum_post_info or {},
    }
    manifest_path.write_text(json.dumps(payload, ensure_ascii=False, indent=2), encoding="utf-8")
    return StageResult(success=True, output_file=str(final_output), artifacts={"manifest_file": str(manifest_path)})

from __future__ import annotations

from dataclasses import dataclass
import os


@dataclass
class VideoPipelineConfig:
    output_dir: str = "output"
    stop_on_error: bool = True
    keep_intermediate_files: bool = False

    @classmethod
    def from_env(cls, output_dir: str) -> "VideoPipelineConfig":
        stop_on_error = os.getenv("CLONECUT_PIPELINE_STOP_ON_ERROR", "true").strip().lower() == "true"
        keep_intermediate = (
            os.getenv("CLONECUT_PIPELINE_KEEP_INTERMEDIATE", "false").strip().lower() == "true"
        )
        return cls(
            output_dir=output_dir,
            stop_on_error=stop_on_error,
            keep_intermediate_files=keep_intermediate,
        )


__all__ = ["VideoPipelineConfig"]

  69:     def run(
  70:         self,
  71:         input_video: str,
  72:         task_id: str,
  73:         start_from_stage: int = 0,
  74:         forum_post_info: Optional[dict] = None,
  75:     ) -> PipelineResult:
  76:         current = input_video
  77:         executed: List[str] = []
  78:         stage_start = max(0, int(start_from_stage))
  79:         context: Dict[str, Any] = {"forum_post_info": _normalize_forum_post_info(forum_post_info)}
  80:         last_stage_index = max(0, min(stage_start, len(self._stages) - 1 if self._stages else 0))
  81:         last_stage_name: Optional[str] = None
  82:         gpu_stage_indexes = {1, 2, 4, 6}
  83:         tracking_started = False
  84: 
  85:         if self.performance_tracker is not None:
  86:             try:
  87:                 path = Path(input_video)
  88:                 file_size_mb = 0.0
  89:                 if path.exists():
  90:                     file_size_mb = path.stat().st_size / (1024 * 1024)
  91:                 duration_seconds = probe_duration_seconds(input_video)
  92:                 self.performance_tracker.start_video_processing(
  93:                     task_id=task_id,
  94:                     video_filename=path.name,
  95:                     original_filename=path.name,
  96:                     file_size_mb=file_size_mb,
  97:                     video_duration_seconds=duration_seconds,
  98:                 )
  99:                 tracking_started = True
 100:             except Exception as exc:
 101:                 self.logger.warning("start performance tracking failed: task=%s err=%s", task_id, exc)
 102: 
 103:         for idx, (stage_name, handler) in enumerate(self._stages):
 104:             if idx < stage_start:
 105:                 continue
 106: 
 107:             if self.resource_monitor is not None:
 108:                 try:
 109:                     self.resource_monitor.record_step_resource(
 110:                         step_num=idx,
 111:                         step_name=stage_name,
 112:                         task_id=task_id,
 113:                     )
 114:                 except Exception as exc:
 115:                     self.logger.debug("resource snapshot failed: task=%s stage=%s err=%s", task_id, stage_name, exc)
 116:             if self.performance_tracker is not None:
 117:                 try:
 118:                     self.performance_tracker.start_stage(
 119:                         task_id=task_id,
 120:                         stage_name=stage_name,
 121:                         gpu_accelerated=(idx in gpu_stage_indexes),
 122:                     )
 123:                 except Exception:
 124:                     pass
 125:             try:
 126:                 result = handler(current, task_id=task_id, stage_name=stage_name, context=context)
 127:             except Exception as exc:
 128:                 if self.performance_tracker is not None:
 129:                     try:
 130:                         self.performance_tracker.end_stage(
 131:                             task_id=task_id,
 132:                             stage_name=stage_name,
 133:                             success=False,
 134:                             error_message=str(exc),
 135:                         )
 136:                         self.performance_tracker.add_error(task_id, str(exc))
 137:                     except Exception:
 138:                         pass
 139:                 perf_report = self._finish_tracking(task_id, tracking_started)
 140:                 return PipelineResult(
 141:                     success=False,
 142:                     output_file=current,
 143:                     error_message=f"{stage_name} exception: {exc}",
 144:                     executed_stages=executed,
 145:                     current_stage=idx,
 146:                     last_stage=last_stage_name,
 147:                     failed_stage=stage_name,
 148:                     performance_report=perf_report,
 149:                 )
 150: 
 151:             executed.append(stage_name)
 152:             last_stage_index = idx
 153:             last_stage_name = stage_name
 154:             if not result.success:
 155:                 if self.performance_tracker is not None:
 156:                     try:
 157:                         self.performance_tracker.end_stage(
 158:                             task_id=task_id,
 159:                             stage_name=stage_name,
 160:                             success=False,
 161:                             error_message=str(result.error_message or ""),
 162:                         )
 163:                         self.performance_tracker.add_error(
 164:                             task_id,
 165:                             str(result.error_message or f"{stage_name} failed"),
 166:                         )
 167:                     except Exception:
 168:                         pass
 169:                 perf_report = self._finish_tracking(task_id, tracking_started)
 170:                 return PipelineResult(
 171:                     success=False,

 181:                 try:
 182:                     self.performance_tracker.end_stage(
 183:                         task_id=task_id,
 184:                         stage_name=stage_name,
 185:                         success=True,
 186:                     )
 187:                 except Exception:
 188:                     pass
 189:             if result.output_file:
 190:                 current = result.output_file

 192:         perf_report = self._finish_tracking(task_id, tracking_started)
 193:         summary = f"internal pipeline executed stages={len(executed)}"
 194:         if perf_report is not None:
 195:             try:
 196:                 ratio = float(getattr(perf_report, "processing_speed_ratio", 0.0))
 197:                 if ratio > 0:
 198:                     summary = f"internal pipeline executed stages={len(executed)} speed={ratio:.2f}x"
 199:             except Exception:
 200:                 pass
 201:         return PipelineResult(
 202:             success=True,
 203:             output_file=current,
 204:             executed_stages=executed,
 205:             performance_summary=summary,
 206:             current_stage=last_stage_index,
 207:             last_stage=last_stage_name,
 208:             performance_report=perf_report,
 209:         )

 211:     def _finish_tracking(self, task_id: str, tracking_started: bool) -> Optional[Any]:
 212:         if not tracking_started or self.performance_tracker is None:
 213:             return None
 214:         try:
 215:             return self.performance_tracker.end_video_processing(task_id)
 216:         except Exception:
 217:             return None

 298: 
 299: def _normalize_forum_post_info(raw: Optional[dict]) -> Dict[str, Any]:
 300:     if not isinstance(raw, dict):
 301:         return {}
 302: 
 303:     info: Dict[str, Any] = dict(raw)
 304:     hotwords = _normalize_hotwords(info.get("hotwords"))
 305:     info["hotwords"] = hotwords
 306: 
 307:     speaker = _pick_first_text(
 308:         info,
 309:         keys=("speaker", "speaker_id", "spk", "target_speaker"),
 310:     )
 311:     if speaker:
 312:         info["speaker"] = speaker
 313: 
 314:     cover_titles = _normalize_cover_titles(info.get("cover_titles"))
 315:     cover_up = _pick_first_text(info, keys=("cover_title_up", "灏侀潰鏍囬涓?))
 316:     cover_middle = _pick_first_text(info, keys=("cover_title_middle", "灏侀潰鏍囬涓?))
 317:     cover_down = _pick_first_text(info, keys=("cover_title_down", "灏侀潰鏍囬涓?))
 318: 
 319:     if not cover_up and len(cover_titles) >= 1:
 320:         cover_up = cover_titles[0]
 321:     if not cover_middle and len(cover_titles) >= 2:
 322:         cover_middle = cover_titles[1]
 323:     if not cover_down and len(cover_titles) >= 3:
 324:         cover_down = cover_titles[2]
 325: 
 326:     compact_titles = [item for item in (cover_up, cover_middle, cover_down) if item]
 327:     if compact_titles:
 328:         cover_titles = compact_titles
 329: 
 330:     info["cover_title_up"] = cover_up
 331:     info["cover_title_middle"] = cover_middle
 332:     info["cover_title_down"] = cover_down
 333:     info["灏侀潰鏍囬涓?] = cover_up
 334:     info["灏侀潰鏍囬涓?] = cover_middle
 335:     info["灏侀潰鏍囬涓?] = cover_down
 336:     info["cover_titles"] = cover_titles
 337: 
 338:     return info
 339: 
 340: 
 341: def _normalize_cover_titles(value: Any) -> List[str]:
 342:     if not isinstance(value, list):
 343:         return []
 344:     output: List[str] = []
 345:     seen: set[str] = set()
 346:     for item in value:
 347:         if isinstance(item, dict):
 348:             text = str(item.get("text", "")).strip()
 349:         else:
 350:             text = str(item or "").strip()
 351:         normalized = " ".join(text.split())
 352:         if not normalized:
 353:             continue
 354:         if normalized in seen:
 355:             continue
 356:         seen.add(normalized)
 357:         output.append(normalized)
 358:         if len(output) >= 3:
 359:             break
 360:     return output
 361: 
 362: 
 363: def _normalize_hotwords(value: Any) -> List[str]:
 364:     candidates: List[str] = []
 365:     if isinstance(value, list):
 366:         candidates = [str(item).strip() for item in value]
 367:     elif isinstance(value, str):
 368:         candidates = [item.strip() for item in value.replace("\uFF0C", ",").split(",")]
 369: 
 370:     output: List[str] = []
 371:     seen: set[str] = set()
 372:     for item in candidates:
 373:         text = str(item or "").strip()
 374:         if not text:
 375:             continue
 376:         dedup_key = text.lower()
 377:         if dedup_key in seen:
 378:             continue
 379:         seen.add(dedup_key)
 380:         output.append(text)
 381:     return output
 382: 
 383: 
 384: def _pick_first_text(info: Dict[str, Any], keys: tuple[str, ...]) -> str:
 385:     for key in keys:
 386:         value = str(info.get(key, "")).strip()
 387:         if value:
 388:             return value
 389:     return ""
 390: 
 391: 
 392: __all__ = ["VideoPipeline", "VideoPipelineConfig", "PipelineResult"]

from __future__ import annotations

import json
from pathlib import Path

from domain.video.stages import stage4_asr, stage5_ai_text


def test_stage4_prefers_sidecar_subtitle(monkeypatch, tmp_path) -> None:  # type: ignore[no-untyped-def]
    monkeypatch.setenv("CLONECUT_ASR_BACKEND", "sidecar")
    source = tmp_path / "input.mp4"
    source.write_bytes(b"fake-video")
    sidecar = tmp_path / "input.srt"
    sidecar.write_text(
        "\n".join(
            [
                "1",
                "00:00:00,000 --> 00:00:01,500",
                "hello world",
                "",
                "2",
                "00:00:01,500 --> 00:00:03,000",
                "second line",
                "",
            ]
        ),
        encoding="utf-8",
    )

    out_dir = tmp_path / "out"
    result = stage4_asr.run(input_video=str(source), output_dir=str(out_dir), task_id="v1")
    assert result.success
    assert result.output_file
    assert Path(str(result.output_file)).exists()

    srt = out_dir / "v1" / "_stages" / "v1_stage4_asr_subtitles.srt"
    transcript = out_dir / "v1" / "_stages" / "v1_stage4_asr_transcript.txt"
    manifest = out_dir / "v1" / "_stages" / "v1_stage4_asr_manifest.json"
    assert srt.exists()
    assert transcript.exists()
    assert manifest.exists()
    assert "hello world" in srt.read_text(encoding="utf-8")
    payload = json.loads(manifest.read_text(encoding="utf-8"))
    assert payload.get("engine") == "sidecar_srt"
    assert payload.get("fallback_used") is False
    attempts = payload.get("attempts") or []
    assert attempts and attempts[0].get("backend") == "sidecar"

def test_stage5_rule_based_script_generation(monkeypatch, tmp_path) -> None:  # type: ignore[no-untyped-def]
    monkeypatch.delenv("OPENAI_API_KEY", raising=False)
    monkeypatch.delenv("CLONECUT_STAGE5_LLM_MODEL", raising=False)

    source = tmp_path / "input.mp4"
    source.write_bytes(b"fake-video")
    out_dir = tmp_path / "out"
    stage_dir = out_dir / "v2" / "_stages"
    stage_dir.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
    srt = stage_dir / "v2_stage4_asr_subtitles.srt"
    srt.write_text(
        "\n".join(
            [
                "1",
                "00:00:00,000 --> 00:00:02,000",
                "build a clear workflow",
                "",
                "2",
                "00:00:02,000 --> 00:00:04,000",
                "validate every stage with tests",
                "",
            ]
        ),
        encoding="utf-8",
    )

    result = stage5_ai_text.run(input_video=str(source), output_dir=str(out_dir), task_id="v2")
    assert result.success
    assert result.output_file
    assert Path(str(result.output_file)).exists()

    script = stage_dir / "v2_stage5_ai_script.txt"
    manifest = stage_dir / "v2_stage5_ai_manifest.json"
    pointer = stage_dir / "v2_stage5_script_path.txt"
    assert script.exists()
    assert manifest.exists()
    assert pointer.exists()

    content = script.read_text(encoding="utf-8")
    assert "Script Draft" in content
    assert "Key Points:" in content
    payload = json.loads(manifest.read_text(encoding="utf-8"))
    assert payload.get("engine") == "rule_based"

            return False, "No NVENC capable devices found"
        return True, ""

    monkeypatch.setattr(stage2_silence, "run_ffmpeg", fake_run_ffmpeg)

    assert error == ""
    assert len(captured) == 2
    codecs = [cmd[cmd.index("-c:v") + 1] for cmd in captured]
    assert codecs == ["h264_nvenc", "libx264"]

    srt = stage_dir / f"{task_id}_stage6_5_resub_subtitles.srt"
    ass = stage_dir / f"{task_id}_stage6_5_resub_subtitles.ass"
    srt.write_text(
        "\n".join(
            [
                "1",
                "00:00:00,000 --> 00:00:01,000",
                "hello srt",
                "",
            ]
        ),
        encoding="utf-8",
    )
    ass.write_text(
        "\n".join(
            [
                "[Script Info]",
                "Title: ass subtitle",
                "",
                "[Events]",
                "Format: Layer, Start, End, Style, Name, MarginL, MarginR, MarginV, Effect, Text",
                "Dialogue: 0,0:00:00.00,0:00:01.00,Default,,0,0,0,,hello ass",
            ]
        ),
        encoding="utf-8",
    )

    monkeypatch.setenv("CLONECUT_STAGE7_MODE", "burn")
    monkeypatch.setattr(stage7_subtitle, "ffmpeg_exists", lambda: True)
    captured = {"cmd": []}

    def fake_run_ffmpeg(args, timeout_seconds=1800):  # type: ignore[no-untyped-def]
        captured["cmd"] = list(args)
        Path(args[-1]).write_bytes(b"burned-video")
        return True, ""

    monkeypatch.setattr(stage7_subtitle, "run_ffmpeg", fake_run_ffmpeg)
    result = stage7_subtitle.run(input_video=str(source), output_dir=str(out_dir), task_id=task_id)
    assert result.success
    vf_expr = captured["cmd"][captured["cmd"].index("-vf") + 1]
    assert vf_expr.startswith("ass=")

    assert "between(t,0,1.700)" in filter_expr

def test_build_clip_ranges_respects_max_duration(monkeypatch, tmp_path) -> None:  # type: ignore[no-untyped-def]
    monkeypatch.delenv("CLONECUT_STAGE6_PAD_BEFORE_SECONDS", raising=False)
    monkeypatch.delenv("CLONECUT_STAGE6_PAD_AFTER_SECONDS", raising=False)
    monkeypatch.delenv("CLONECUT_STAGE6_MERGE_GAP_SECONDS", raising=False)
    monkeypatch.delenv("CLONECUT_STAGE6_MIN_CLIP_SECONDS", raising=False)
    monkeypatch.delenv("CLONECUT_STAGE6_MAX_SEGMENTS", raising=False)

    subtitle = tmp_path / "sample.srt"
    subtitle.write_text(
        "\n".join(
            [
                "1",
                "00:00:00,000 --> 00:00:01,000",
                "line a",
                "",
                "2",
                "00:00:03,000 --> 00:00:04,000",
                "line b",
                "",
                "3",
                "00:00:08,000 --> 00:00:09,000",
                "line c",
                "",
            ]
        ),
        encoding="utf-8",
    )

    ranges, detail = stage6_clip._build_clip_ranges(  # type: ignore[attr-defined]
        subtitle_path=subtitle,
        video_duration=12.0,
        max_duration=3,
    )
    assert ranges
    total = sum(max(0.0, end - start) for start, end in ranges)
    assert total <= 3.01
    assert "merged=" in detail

def test_stage6_trim_gpu_codec_failure_downgrades_to_libx264(monkeypatch, tmp_path) -> None:  # type: ignore[no-untyped-def]
    source = tmp_path / "input.mp4"
    target = tmp_path / "out.mp4"
    source.write_bytes(b"input-video")
    monkeypatch.setenv("CLONECUT_STAGE6_VIDEO_CODEC", "h264_nvenc")

    captured: list[list[str]] = []
    calls = {"count": 0}

    def fake_run_ffmpeg(args, timeout_seconds=1800):  # type: ignore[no-untyped-def]
        captured.append(list(args))
        calls["count"] += 1
        if calls["count"] == 1:
            return False, "No NVENC capable devices found"
        return True, ""

    monkeypatch.setattr(stage6_clip, "run_ffmpeg", fake_run_ffmpeg)
    ok, error = stage6_clip._render_trim_seconds(source=source, target=target, target_seconds=3.0)  # type: ignore[attr-defined]

    assert ok is True
    assert error == ""
    codecs = [cmd[cmd.index("-c:v") + 1] for cmd in captured]
    assert codecs == ["h264_nvenc", "libx264"]


def test_build_clip_ranges_supports_speaker_filter(tmp_path) -> None:  # type: ignore[no-untyped-def]
    subtitle = tmp_path / "sample.srt"
    subtitle.write_text(
        "\n".join(
            [
                "1",
                "00:00:00,000 --> 00:00:01,000",
                "[spk-A] line a",
                "",
                "2",
                "00:00:02,000 --> 00:00:03,000",
                "[spk-B] line b",
                "",
                "3",
                "00:00:04,000 --> 00:00:05,000",
                "[spk-A] line c",
                "",
            ]
        ),
        encoding="utf-8",
    )

    ranges, detail = stage6_clip._build_clip_ranges(  # type: ignore[attr-defined]
        subtitle_path=subtitle,
        video_duration=8.0,
        max_duration=0,
        target_speaker="spk-A",
    )
    assert len(ranges) == 2
    assert "speaker_filter target=spk-A matched=2/3" in detail


def test_stage6_clip_fallback_when_ffmpeg_missing(monkeypatch, tmp_path) -> None:  # type: ignore[no-untyped-def]
    monkeypatch.setattr(stage6_clip, "ffmpeg_exists", lambda: False)
    source = tmp_path / "input.mp4"
    source.write_bytes(b"fake-video")

    out_dir = tmp_path / "out"
    result = stage6_clip.run(input_video=str(source), output_dir=str(out_dir), task_id="v6")
    assert result.success
    assert result.output_file
    output_path = Path(str(result.output_file))
    assert output_path.exists()
    assert output_path.name.endswith("stage6_clip_copy.mp4")

    manifest_path = out_dir / "v6" / "_stages" / "v6_stage6_clip_manifest.json"
    assert manifest_path.exists()
    payload = json.loads(manifest_path.read_text(encoding="utf-8"))
    assert payload.get("method") == "copy_fallback"


def test_stage6_clip_strict_mode_rejects_copy_fallback(monkeypatch, tmp_path) -> None:  # type: ignore[no-untyped-def]
    monkeypatch.setenv("CLONECUT_STRICT_EQUIVALENCE", "true")
    monkeypatch.setattr(stage6_clip, "ffmpeg_exists", lambda: False)
    source = tmp_path / "input.mp4"
    source.write_bytes(b"fake-video")

    out_dir = tmp_path / "out"
    result = stage6_clip.run(input_video=str(source), output_dir=str(out_dir), task_id="v6_strict")
    assert result.success is False
    assert "strict equivalence" in str(result.error_message)

    manifest_path = out_dir / "v6_strict" / "_stages" / "v6_strict_stage6_clip_manifest.json"
    payload = json.loads(manifest_path.read_text(encoding="utf-8"))
    assert payload.get("method") == "strict_rejected"
    assert payload.get("fallback_used") is True


def test_stage6_clip_can_trim_with_duration_guide_path(monkeypatch, tmp_path) -> None:  # type: ignore[no-untyped-def]
    source = tmp_path / "input.mp4"
    source.write_bytes(b"input-video")
    guide_video = tmp_path / "guide.mp4"
    guide_video.write_bytes(b"guide-video")
    monkeypatch.setenv("CLONECUT_STAGE6_DURATION_GUIDE_PATH", str(guide_video))
    monkeypatch.setattr(stage6_clip, "ffmpeg_exists", lambda: True)
    monkeypatch.setattr(
        stage6_clip,
        "probe_duration_seconds",
        lambda path: 12.3 if str(path).endswith("guide.mp4") else 30.0,
    )

    def fake_run_ffmpeg(args, timeout_seconds=1800):  # type: ignore[no-untyped-def]
        out = Path(args[-1])
        out.parent.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
        out.write_bytes(b"trimmed-video")
        return True, ""

    monkeypatch.setattr(stage6_clip, "run_ffmpeg", fake_run_ffmpeg)

    out_dir = tmp_path / "out"
    result = stage6_clip.run(input_video=str(source), output_dir=str(out_dir), task_id="v6_guide")
    assert result.success
    assert result.output_file
    output_path = Path(str(result.output_file))
    assert output_path.exists()
    assert output_path.read_bytes() == b"trimmed-video"

    manifest_path = out_dir / "v6_guide" / "_stages" / "v6_guide_stage6_clip_manifest.json"
    payload = json.loads(manifest_path.read_text(encoding="utf-8"))
    assert payload.get("method") == "duration_guide_trim"


def test_stage6_clip_text_match(monkeypatch, tmp_path) -> None:  # type: ignore[no-untyped-def]
    source = tmp_path / "input.mp4"
    source.write_bytes(b"input-video")
    clip_text = tmp_path / "clip_text.txt"
    clip_text.write_text("alpha line#gamma line", encoding="utf-8")
    monkeypatch.setenv("CLONECUT_STAGE6_CLIP_TEXT_PATH", str(clip_text))
    monkeypatch.setenv("CLONECUT_STAGE6_CLIP_TEXT_MATCH", "true")
    monkeypatch.setenv("CLONECUT_STAGE6_CLIP_TEXT_MIN_SCORE", "0.4")
    monkeypatch.setattr(stage6_clip, "ffmpeg_exists", lambda: True)
    monkeypatch.setattr(stage6_clip, "probe_duration_seconds", lambda _: 10.0)

    def fake_run_ffmpeg(args, timeout_seconds=1800):  # type: ignore[no-untyped-def]
        out = Path(args[-1])
        out.parent.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
        out.write_bytes(b"segment-or-concat")
        return True, ""

    monkeypatch.setattr(stage6_clip, "run_ffmpeg", fake_run_ffmpeg)

    out_dir = tmp_path / "out"
    stage_dir = out_dir / "v6_native" / "_stages"
    stage_dir.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
    subtitle = stage_dir / "v6_native_stage4_asr_subtitles.srt"
    subtitle.write_text(
        "\n".join(
            [
                "1",
                "00:00:00,000 --> 00:00:01,000",
                "alpha line",
                "",
                "2",
                "00:00:03,000 --> 00:00:04,000",
                "beta line",
                "",
                "3",
                "00:00:06,000 --> 00:00:07,000",
                "gamma line",
                "",
            ]
        ),
        encoding="utf-8",
    )

    result = stage6_clip.run(input_video=str(source), output_dir=str(out_dir), task_id="v6_native")
    assert result.success
    assert result.output_file
    output_path = Path(str(result.output_file))
    assert output_path.exists()
    assert output_path.read_bytes() == b"segment-or-concat"

    manifest_path = out_dir / "v6_native" / "_stages" / "v6_native_stage6_clip_manifest.json"
    payload = json.loads(manifest_path.read_text(encoding="utf-8"))
    assert payload.get("method") == "subtitle_clip_text_concat"


def test_stage6_clip_uses_stage4_manifest_speaker_filter(monkeypatch, tmp_path) -> None:  # type: ignore[no-untyped-def]
    source = tmp_path / "input.mp4"
    source.write_bytes(b"input-video")
    monkeypatch.setattr(stage6_clip, "ffmpeg_exists", lambda: True)
    monkeypatch.setattr(stage6_clip, "probe_duration_seconds", lambda _: 8.0)

    def fake_run_ffmpeg(args, timeout_seconds=1800):  # type: ignore[no-untyped-def]
        out = Path(args[-1])
        out.parent.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
        out.write_bytes(b"segment-or-concat")
        return True, ""

    monkeypatch.setattr(stage6_clip, "run_ffmpeg", fake_run_ffmpeg)

    out_dir = tmp_path / "out"
    stage_dir = out_dir / "v6_spk" / "_stages"
    stage_dir.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)

            [

                "",

                "00:00:03,000 --> 00:00:04,000",

                "",

        ),
        encoding="utf-8",

from __future__ import annotations

from pathlib import Path
from types import SimpleNamespace

from apps.gradio_ui.backend import GradioBackend, GradioBackendConfig


def test_gradio_backend_run_asr_clip_subtitle_manual_chain(monkeypatch, tmp_path) -> None:  # type: ignore[no-untyped-def]
    source = tmp_path / "demo.mp4"
    source.write_bytes(b"video")

    backend = GradioBackend(GradioBackendConfig(output_dir=str(tmp_path / "out")))

    calls = {"asr": 0, "clip": 0, "sub": 0}

    def fake_stage4(input_video, output_dir, task_id, forum_post_info=None, hotwords=None, speaker=None):  # type: ignore[no-untyped-def]
        calls["asr"] += 1
        assert Path(input_video).exists()
        assert output_dir == str(tmp_path / "out")
        assert isinstance(hotwords, list)
        return SimpleNamespace(success=True, output_file=str(source), error_message=None)

    def fake_stage6(input_video, output_dir, task_id):  # type: ignore[no-untyped-def]
        calls["clip"] += 1
        return SimpleNamespace(success=True, output_file=str(source), error_message=None)

    def fake_stage65(input_video, output_dir, task_id):  # type: ignore[no-untyped-def]
        calls["sub"] += 1
        return SimpleNamespace(success=True, output_file=str(source), error_message=None)

    monkeypatch.setattr("apps.gradio_ui.backend.run_stage4_asr", fake_stage4)
    monkeypatch.setattr("apps.gradio_ui.backend.run_stage6_clip", fake_stage6)
    monkeypatch.setattr("apps.gradio_ui.backend.run_stage6_5_resub", fake_stage65)

    asr = backend.run_asr(str(source), hotwords="热词A,热词B", speaker="spk1")
    assert asr["success"] is True

    clip = backend.run_clip(str(source), clip_text="第一句\n第二句", speaker="spk1")
    assert clip["success"] is True

    subtitle = backend.run_subtitle(str(source), subtitle_format="ass")
    assert subtitle["success"] is True

    chain = backend.run_manual_chain(
        str(source),
        hotwords="热词A,热词B",
        clip_text="第一句",
        speaker="spk1",
        subtitle_format="ass",
    )
    assert chain["success"] is True
    assert calls["asr"] >= 2
    assert calls["clip"] >= 2
    assert calls["sub"] >= 2


def test_gradio_backend_handles_missing_input_file(tmp_path) -> None:  # type: ignore[no-untyped-def]
    backend = GradioBackend(GradioBackendConfig(output_dir=str(tmp_path / "out")))

    result = backend.run_asr(str(tmp_path / "missing.mp4"))
    assert result["success"] is False
    assert "not found" in str(result.get("error", ""))

Minor

- There is generated noise in the worktree (clonecut.egg-info/) unrelated to the stage skeleton. It is not a code bug, but it weakens change isolation for a task that should stay focused on domain/video/.

Assessment

This is a good minimal skeleton for the very narrow acceptance bar of “make domain.video.VideoPipeline import and let tests/unit/test_video_pipeline.py pass.” It is not yet a clean repo-quality Task 1 change, because it restores one path by breaking or masking other established stage contracts.

If you want Task 2 to be easier, I would require one of these before sign-off: add thin compatibility shims now (run aliases, stage_artifact_path, minimal manifest-name stability), or explicitly delete/quarantine the old direct stage consumers and update the affected tests in the same phase.

The Gradio tests pass because they monkeypatch backend symbols after import rather than exercising the real import bindings ([test_gradio_backend.py:13](C:/Users/ai/.config/superpowers/worktrees/clonecut/codex-video-pipeline-startup-20260328/tests/unit/test_gradio_backend.py#L13), [backend.py:10](C:/Users/ai/.config/superpowers/worktrees/clonecut/codex-video-pipeline-startup-20260328/apps/gradio_ui/backend.py#L10)). That hides regressions instead of surfacing them.

Minor

- There is generated noise in the worktree (clonecut.egg-info/) unrelated to the stage skeleton. It is not a code bug, but it weakens change isolation for a task that should stay focused on domain/video/.

Assessment

This is a good minimal skeleton for the very narrow acceptance bar of “make domain.video.VideoPipeline import and let tests/unit/test_video_pipeline.py pass.” It is not yet a clean repo-quality Task 1 change, because it restores one path by breaking or masking other established stage contracts.

If you want Task 2 to be easier, I would require one of these before sign-off: add thin compatibility shims now (run aliases, stage_artifact_path, minimal manifest-name stability), or explicitly delete/quarantine the old direct stage consumers and update the affected tests in the same phase.
